This feature is enabled when the option \"Enable track route on map\" in the settings menu is not checked. When you stop the function clicking on \"Stop follow me\", the route will not be stored in the device. This way, if you go from point B to point A, you can follow a route on map previously stored and loaded (follow back).\r\n\r\n4) Replay route on the map (a route previously stored in step 2).
